<date>1583784735451<//date>< Review>
I needed some front repair work done to the frame of my car so that it could pass the brake and light inspection that it previously failed. Since I only had 30 days to do a retest, I was extremely worried that I would not find a shop to be able to do the work in time for me to pay my registration. When I called, Doug said he would take a look at my car and that he was sure that he could squeeze me in. Sure enough, I was able to buy my parts and get into the shop the very next week. The customer service (Doug especially) was awesome, and the end results were quite pleasing, though I had a few slight concerns with other parts of service.

My two concerns were:
1. I was never given a quote for how much the work would cost. I was kinda shocked at how much it was went I went to check out, but saw the cost breakdown and it made sense afterwards, but still left me reeling a bit (especially as a poor college student)
2. They had taken the panels of the sides of my trunk to put in my new brake/tail marker lights but never put them back on, so I had to re-install the panels

Overall, the work was really good. I saw immediately that it looked 10x better in the front than before. And I was able to pass my re-inspection with flying colors. Thanks again, Doug and team.< /Review>

< text>
5 stars for fried artichokes and friendliness. The actual store is... Weird. Looks like it is out of business when you walk in or something. But the fried artichokes were delicious - best I've ever had at least. They're actual artichoke hearts, not from a jar, and because of that they have a very different taste. There really isn't much spices or seasoning with them - so i suppose i could see then being called watery. The long reigning champion of fried artichokes previous to these were very seasoned. I love them both for different reasons, but ultimately these take the win. They're just so meaty and good dipped in ranch. Mmmm, go get some. They do appear to have upped the prices though - $12.50 for 30 pieces. Totally worth it though<//text>

If you're in the area this is a must stop for any artichoke lover. Don't even bother with the restaurant next door. The Fruit & Veg Stand has antiquate seating and you can order directly from the counter. You will not find better prices anywhere for fried artichoke hearts period. As of July 2013 you could grab a 20 piece with 2 dippings for 6.50 or a 30 piece for 9.50.  These are the largest artichoke hearts you will find anywhere on planet earth and they come out hot and fresh. I'll end this review now since I'm beginning to drool on my keyboard.< /Review>

<rating>5</rating><Review>Great workouts for those who don't like the same routine workouts!

I joined the 6 week challenge like many others which did require the $499 deposit and to meet either goals of losing 5% body fat or 25lbs. I think the hardest part of the challenge was probably the diet plans because it really required a lifestyle change, and it really made me aware of what I was putting in my body. Their meal plan is very straightforward, but you really do want to workout everyday regardless of the minimum 3 times a week class workout to meet the challenge. I focused on cardio and going to the classes which are super fun! You do it at your own pace but you get more out of it by challenging yourself. It was awesome to see myself being able to slowly follow the class at a better pace and I definitely felt myself having more energy throughout the day as well. They vary the warm up circuits and boxing rounds which make each class different! It's definitely important to try to book the class ahead of time since they do book up quite quickly!

<text>It's a great place to hangout. The senior center provides lots of things to do.  Monday  is classic movie day. Weds  is bingo
Fridays is new movies.  Special luncheon for only $3. Free hair cuts. They have crafts, computer,  library  billards,  a gym, many other classes. A person can get the senior bus. Be left off and picked up. You could buy lunch or breakfast on certain days. You can also bring your own.  The center also sells coffee and snacks for less than 50 cents. They also offer excursions . You can read all about them in the Riverside parks & recreation magazine. The senior center is a great place to meet people and get social. The staff and volunteers are helpful and friendly.  Once a month the center gives out a bag or two of food items for free. The program is called food share
In the summer there is air conditioning.  In the winter there is heat. Come on down. Seniors in Riverside means 55 and up of age. No one has a time limit of how long you could hangout.  At least until closing.<//text><pics>None</pics>< Response>

< Review>
Great friendly little bar on base. They have free pizza during "happy hour". I my case it was not free. It was the first place I found after arriving on a Space A flight and checking into my room. Don't be a rookie like me and walk in with a baseball cap (hat) or you will hear cheers and a bell ring. Next thing you know your buying a round for the bar. Thankfully, when I entered only four people where at the bar. The round was $32.00 with tip. Four new friends, great conversation and several slices of pizza (to try to make up for the loss).

They also have rules against putting a cell phone on the bar (almost got me on that one also) & touching any of the model aircraft hanging from the ceiling so be careful.

Hey, I am retired Air Force what do I know about crazy Navy rules. It was all good.</Review>

Dropped in yesterday with a problem with sluggish running on my 2013 FLSTC. We were on the road from San Diego to Yuma and didn't want to risk a breakdown in the desert.

<name>Ron Rogers</name><Pics>None<//Pics><text>I have been using Sweetwater since long before they were in this building. I have been riding for over 50 years and can tell you there is no perfect bike shop! However, if you want a shop you can develop a personal relationship with, depend on to make it right if something goes wrong, and have the best prices, I would recommend Sweetwater!  Unlike other Harley shops, many if not most employees stay here. Also, it has been my experience that, if I find an item cheaper at another Harley shop, they match the price. As for the shop, I have to remember that not every mechanical or electrical problem is easily diagnosed and sometimes is seems there is a gremlin living in the older bikes, (just sold my 97 Road King with over 100K on it). To the best of my knowledge they always stand behind their work.
In summery I will say this is a great locals Harley shop, just like the shops of old when we depended on word of mouth and not advertising to locate a reliable Harley Shop. Spend some time there, ask their names and call them by name when you return.

I bought a 2014 Low Rider last year on Halloween from these guys.  Leading up to my buy I visited all the H-D dealers in the area; SD, El Cajon, and Sweetwater.  I live in Chula.  Sweetwater was by far the best and knows how to do business.  I took maybe 2 months to buy a bike and really appreciated not being sold to. <user>103143752457591932675<//user>< name>
Dave Leake< /name>
<Date>1414205926495<//Date><Rating>5</Rating><Review>I brought my bike in for a service a week ago. After getting ready to roll for the weekend, I noticed a strange noise coming from the primary. I suspected it was due to something that may have happened, or been missed, during the service.

I called the service department and the manager, Charles, had me bring the bike in for a look-hear. Andy, the technician who conducted the service on my bike last week, was brought out to listen to my bike. He immediately identified it as a loose compensator nut (if any of you have ever heard this noise, it is horrible. I've likened it to the sound to one of those small pull back toys you had as a kid when you would pull the car back and, instead of letting it go on the floor, pick the toy up and let the tires rip out in the air). I had had this exact noise a few years back and recognized it again after he stated the problem. I can't believe I didn't recognize it myself.

Not wanting to miss my weekend ride, I realized I was now at the whim of the schedule since the issue was not at all related to my prior service. I asked Charles to see if he could get me in...Alfredo said they could get Andy onto my bike the next available time slot. I gladly accepted the offer and prepared to take a taxi back to work.
Upon hearing me mention a Taxi, Alfredo offered to have Marcos drop me off in the SweetWater F150. This saved me a chunk of change... furthermore, Marcos even came back to my work to pick me up and bring my back to pick up my bike. Apparently, this is a free service that SweetWater provides if their drivers are available.

While Andy had the primary cover off, he recommended replacing the Chain Tensioner pad since we were already in there since it was only a $5.00 part and was half worn. This is great advice and preventive maintenance. I believe other technicians may not have been so observant or bothered to recommend the replacement.

Upon paying, Nate advised Alfredo not to forget my military discount and saved me a bit more cash on the gasket.

Thanks guys, so far, I'm glad I selected you to be my dealer of choice while serving in San Diego.
See you further down the road.

SFC David A. Leake< /Review>< Pics>
